**Archives**

## Special Editions Released in 2023

* * *

**This page is provided for archive purposes.** **[Upcoming special editions are available here](https://beautifulbooks.info/finding-fancy-books/special-editions/).**

* * *

[→ Go to the current special editions page](https://beautifulbooks.info/finding-fancy-books/special-editions/)

This page is an archive of “special editions” published in 2023 – a couple are OOP but many are still available to buy, so please enjoy perusing the titles!

Jump to release date:

I deeply appreciate your support of my site if you use these links, but warmly encourage you to buy from your local Indie bookshop if you have the opportunity._

#### December 2023

[![hinrichs narrative design 23](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20205%20300'%3E%3C/svg%3E)](https://beautifulbooks.info/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/hinrichs-narrative-design-23.webp)

##### **Narrative Design** – Kit Hinrichs

Release date: Dec 26, 2023

_“An extraordinary book and unparalleled collection of work, celebrating Kit Hinrichs creative life as he recounts his narrative design work covering over 50 years and all stages of his career.”_

* * *

**_Slipcased Edition_**: US hardback in die-cut slipcase.

➤ **Find it at** [**Amazon**](https://amzn.to/472fs4r) **\| [B&N](https://www.tkqlhce.com/click-100208466-12366831?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.barnesandnoble.com%2Fw%3Fean%3D9781954632172) \| [Waterstones](https://www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=3787&awinaffid=519319&platform=dl&ued=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.waterstones.com%2Fbook%2F9781954632172) \| [Blackwells](https://blackwells.co.uk/bookshop/product/9781954632172?im_ref=Vjhz18VBAxycRqjQ4FzfBXLwUku0p9TZqVy-UU0&sharedid=&irpid=1223186&irgwc=1&afsrc=1)**

##### **Ruthless Vows** – Rebecca Ross

Release date: Dec 26, 2023

“ _The epic conclusion to the intensely romantic and beautifully written story that started in Divine Rivals.”_

* * *

**_B&N Exclusive_**: US hardback with an alternate cover, unique case and case stamp, and special endpapers.

➤ **Find it at** [Barnes & Noble](https://www.kqzyfj.com/click-100208466-12366831?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.barnesandnoble.com%2Fw%2Fruthless-vows-rebecca-ross%2F1143330976%3Fean%3D9781250350923)

##### **The Dark Crystal: Creation Myths, The Complete Collection** – Brian Froud

Release date: Dec 21, 2023

“ _Reveals the definitive origins of the Skeksis, Mystics, Gelfling, and the Dark Crystal itself while introducing all new characters in an epic spanning thousands of years.”_

* * *

**40th Anniversary Collection**: ‘Premium hardcover edition'.

➤ **Find it at** **[Amazon](https://amzn.to/430fZ4I) \| [B&N](https://www.tkqlhce.com/click-100208466-12366831?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.barnesandnoble.com%2Fw%3Fean%3D9781608861217) \| [Blackwells](https://blackwells.co.uk/bookshop/product/9781608861217?im_ref=Vjhz18VBAxycRqjQ4FzfBXLwUku0p9TZqVy-UU0&sharedid=&irpid=1223186&irgwc=1&afsrc=1)**

##### **This Other Eden** – Paul Harding

Release date: Dec 19, 2023

_“This stunning novel, based on actual historical events, will leave readers breathless with its gorgeous prose and unforgettable characters. Harding brings Apple Island to life with his lush descriptions. It is a place and a story that will live on in readers’ minds for years to come.”_

* * *

**B&N Exclusive**: US paperback with a note from the author, along with facsimile pages of his writing notebooks which provide readers with a glimpse of how he developed the novel.

**➤ Find it at [Barnes & Noble](https://www.tkqlhce.com/click-100208466-12366831?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.barnesandnoble.com%2Fw%2Fthis-other-eden-paul-harding%2F1141471394%3Fean%3D9781324079538)**

* * *

##### **My Little Pony** – Sam Maggs, illustrated by Jeremy Whitley & Tony Fleecs

Release date: Dec 12, 2023

_“A story about the children who bought the original My Little Ponies, in a tale full of friendship, magic, and toys.”_

* * *

**40th Anniversary Special**: ‘An anniversary celebration'.

**➤ Find it at [Amazon](https://amzn.to/3Bn8F7R) \| [B&N](https://www.tkqlhce.com/click-100208466-12366831?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.barnesandnoble.com%2Fw%3Fean%3D9798887240244) \| [Waterstones](https://www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=3787&awinaffid=519319&platform=dl&ued=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.waterstones.com%2Fbook%2F9798887240244) \| [Blackwells](https://blackwells.co.uk/bookshop/product/9798887240244?im_ref=Vjhz18VBAxycRqjQ4FzfBXLwUku0p9TZqVy-UU0&sharedid=&irpid=1223186&irgwc=1&afsrc=1)**

##### **Gold** (Plated Prisoner) – Raven Kennedy

Release date: Dec 7, 2023

_“The glittering final chapter of Kennedy's phenomenally popular Plated Prisoner series concludes Auren's incredible journey in the brilliantly reimagined world of King Midas.”_

* * *

**Waterstones Exclusive**: UK hardback signed by the author with sprayed edge (colour TBC).

➤ **Find it at** [**Waterstones**](https://tidd.ly/3ZGjr2M)

[![gaiman anansi boys 2023](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20195%20300'%3E%3C/svg%3E)](https://beautifulbooks.info/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/gaiman-anansi-boys-2023.webp)

##### **Anansi Boys** – Neil Gaiman

Release date: Dec 5, 2023

_“Fat Charlie Nancy goes on an epic journey from South London to the Caribbean to the beginning of the world as his estranged father is revealed to be an African trickster god.”_

* * *

**Deluxe Edition**: Slipcased UK hardback with new contemporary artwork by Monet Alyssa, including black and white chapter artwork, foiled and designed boards, and full-colour illustrated endpapers.

**➤ Find it at [Amazon](https://amzn.to/3tA0LHu) \| [Waterstones](https://www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=3787&awinaffid=519319&platform=dl&ued=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.waterstones.com%2Fbook%2F9781035405299) \| [Blackwells](https://blackwells.co.uk/bookshop/product/9781035405299?im_ref=Vjhz18VBAxycRqjQ4FzfBXLwUku0p9TZqVy-UU0&sharedid=&irpid=1223186&irgwc=1&afsrc=1)**

**➤ Find special signed slipcased edition with art print at [Waterstones](https://tidd.ly/3FpLuM8)**

Nov 28, 2023.

“A warship trapped in a human body is on a quest for revenge.”

**_10th Anniversary Edition_**: US hardback with new cover and illustrated endpapers, a foil stamped case, and a new introduction from the author.

➤ **Find it at [Amazon](https://amzn.to/3v0UghQ)** **\| [B&N](https://www.tkqlhce.com/click-100208466-12366831?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.barnesandnoble.com%2Fw%3Fean%3D9780316574266) \| [Blackwells](https://blackwells.co.uk/bookshop/product/9780316574266?im_ref=Vjhz18VBAxycRqjQ4FzfBXLwUku0p9TZqVy-UU0&sharedid=&irpid=1223186&irgwc=1&afsrc=1)**

##### **To Kill A Shadow –** Katherine Quinn

Nov 28, 2023.

“Britannia meets The Mist–with a touch of Evil Dead–in this illusory fantasy horror about a kingdom left to darkness.”

**_First print run_**: US hardback with purple sprayed page edges.

➤ **Find it at [Amazon](https://amzn.to/453GmYE) \| [B&N](https://www.tkqlhce.com/click-100208466-12366831?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.barnesandnoble.com%2Fw%2Fto-kill-a-shadow-katherine-quinn%2F1142856540%3Fean%3D9781649374318) \| [Blackwells](https://blackwells.co.uk/bookshop/product/To-Kill-a-Shadow-by-Katherine-Quinn/9781649374318?im_ref=Vjhz18VBAxycRqjQ4FzfBXLwUku0p9TZqVy-UU0&sharedid=&irpid=1223186&irgwc=1&afsrc=1)**

[![lore legends SE](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20236%20300'%3E%3C/svg%3E)](https://beautifulbooks.info/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/lore-legends-SE.webp)

##### **Lore & Legends –** Michael Witwer et al

Nov 28, 2023.

“A deluxe special edition of Lore & Legends, an illustrated guide to Dungeons & Dragons' beloved fifth edition.”

**_Special deluxe edition_**: original cover and slipcase illustrations by Hydro74, three gatefold Through the Ages features that showcase how the artwork of several iconic monsters and characters has changed across editions, and a pull-out drawer that doubles as a dice tray. The drawer holds a 24″ x 36″ adventure map of Faerûn illustrated by Jared Blando, an 8″ x 10″ art print of the original fifth edition Starter Set cover artwork by Jaime Jones, and a custom resin d20 die.

➤ **Find it at [Amazon](https://amzn.to/44QVp7D)** **\| [B&N](https://www.tkqlhce.com/click-100208466-12366831?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.barnesandnoble.com%2Fw%3Fean%3D9781984862464) \| [Blackwells](https://blackwells.co.uk/bookshop/product/9781984862464?im_ref=Vjhz18VBAxycRqjQ4FzfBXLwUku0p9TZqVy-UU0&sharedid=&irpid=1223186&irgwc=1&afsrc=1)**

##### **Love & Misadventure** – Lang Leav

Nov 23, 2023.

“The journey from love to heartbreak to finding love again is personal yet universal. Lang Leav’s evocative poetry speaks to the soul of anyone who has travelled along this path.”

**_10th Anniversary Edition:_** Hardback features a special foreword by Lang Leav and highly personal annotations interspersed throughout. Also included are newly colored artworks and a ribbon marker.

[![grendel devil deed](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20254%20300'%3E%3C/svg%3E)](https://beautifulbooks.info/wp-content/uploads/2023/12/grendel-devil-deed.jpg)

##### **Grendel: Devil by the Deed** – Matt Wagner, Brennan Wagner & Dave Lanphear

Nov 21, 2023.

“Matt Wagner returns to the seminal “Devil by the Deed” Hunter Rose story that started the epic, centuries-spanning Grendel saga. In this all-new reimagining of “Devil by the Deed,” Wagner brings his decades of experience and artistry back to the famous narrative that first began his lengthy and illustrious career as a comic-book author.”

**_Master's Edition:_** includes a signed and numbered tip-in sheet featuring stunning never-before-seen art by Matt Wagner and a unique slipcase!

##### **Little Clothbound Classics** – Various Authors

May 25, 2023.

The “Summer” series of titles in Penguin's Little Clothbound Classics collection.

- _The Library of Babel_ – Jorge Luis Borges
- _Death in Midsummer_– Yukio Mishima
- _The Fall –_ Albert Camus
- _Summer –_ Edith Wharton
- _Chess –_ Stefa Zweig
- _Calypso in Heaven –_ Sam Selvon
- _The Imitation of the Rose –_ Clarice Lispector
- _Babylon Revisited –_ F. Scott Fitzgerald
- _My Friend Maigret –_ Georges Simeon
- _The Awakening –_ Kate Chopin
- _Nabokov's Dozen –_ Vladimir Nabokov
- _Bonjour Tristesse –_ Françoise Sagan

**_Little clothbound classics:_** Decorative clothbound covers designed by Coralie Bickford-Smith.

➤ Visit the [**Little Clothbound Classics**](https://beautifulbooks.info/illustratedbibliographies/classic-fiction/penguin-little-clothbound-classics/) page for details on each title

##### **Yellowface** – Rebecca F. Kuang

May 25, 2023

Athena Liu is a literary darling. June Hayward is literally nobody. Who wants stories by basic white girls anyway? But now Athena is dead. And June has her unfinished manuscript.

**_Waterstones exclusive_**: UK hardback, signed by the author with typewriter keys stencilled on black sprayed page edges.

➤ **Find exclusive edition at [Waterstones](https://www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=3787&awinaffid=519319&platform=dl&ued=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.waterstones.com%2Fbook%2Fyellowface%2Fr-f-kuang%2F9780008626372)**

Without their mother, and away from anything familiar, they must take refuge among strangers. Reluctantly, Mr Evans, the grocer, takes them in, with his kind, timid sister, Aunt Lou. But the children find little comfort in his austere home.
